# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repositories (version-pinned mirrors):**

- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api$` filter
- `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` — use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd$` filter

Scope ALL keyword_search/nls_search queries to these repos.
Use the repo name as the `repo` parameter for read_file/go_to_definition/find_references.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

---

**Sourcegraph Repositories:** `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-kubernetes`, `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-client-go`, `github.com/sg-evals/kubernetes-api`, `github.com/sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd`

# Kubernetes v1beta1 to v1 API Storage Version Registration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that register API group storage versions mapping v1beta1 to v1 equivalents. Look for REST storage providers (in pkg/registry/) that define both v1beta1Storage() and v1Storage() methods, the StorageVersion manager interface (in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/), and the ResourceEncodingConfig that controls which GroupVersion is used for etcd storage.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd` (etcd-io/etcd)

## Summary of v1beta1 to v1 API Storage Version Registration

I've identified **10 key files** and **11 core symbols** related to Kubernetes API storage version registration for v1beta1 to v1 migration:

### **Primary REST Storage Providers (with explicit v1beta1 to v1 mapping):**

1. **pkg/registry/authentication/rest/storage_authentication.go** - Implements v1alpha1Storage, v1beta1Storage, and v1Storage methods for authentication APIs
2. **pkg/registry/storage/rest/storage_storage.go** - Implements all three version methods for storage APIs (classes, attachments, CSI drivers)
3. **pkg/registry/admissionregistration/rest/storage_apiserver.go** - Implements all three version methods for admission policies and webhooks

### **Core Interfaces & Infrastructure:**

4. **StorageVersionProvider** interface (rest.go) - Allows storage objects to disclose their storage version
5. **ResourceEncodingConfig** interface (resource_encoding_config.go) - Controls which GroupVersion is used for etcd storage
6. **DefaultResourceEncodingConfig** struct - Manages resource-specific encoding overrides
7. **StorageFactory & DefaultStorageFactory** - Locates and configures storage for GroupResources

### **Configuration Chain:**

8. **NewStorageFactoryConfig** (default_storage_factory_builder.go) - Establishes ResourceEncodingOverrides for non-latest version storage
9. **MergeResourceEncodingConfigs** (resourceconfig/helpers.go) - Merges default and override configurations
10. **Additional context** from networking and core API groups showing alternative patterns

The architecture enables gradual API version migrations where newer versions can be introduced while older versions remain accessible

as REST storage providers:\\n1. **pkg/registry/authentication/rest/storage_authentication.go** - Registers authentication APIs with v1alpha1Storage, v1beta1Storage, and v1Storage methods, supporting NewRESTStorage() orchestrates calls to version-specific storage methods and populates apiGroupInfo.VersionedResourcesStorageMap accordingly.\\n\\n## Storage Version Management Interface\\nThe **StorageVersionProvider** interface (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/registry/rest/rest.go, line 376-382) is implemented by storage objects to disclose their storage version. The interface's StorageVersion() method returns a runtime.GroupVersioner that outputs the GVK that objects will be converted to before persistence in etcd.\\n\\n## Resource Encoding Configuration\\nThe **ResourceEncodingConfig** interface (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go, line 28-36) controls which GroupVersion is used for etcd storage.
